***gegrond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegrond.html>gegrond</a> (33388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gegrond.html>gegrond</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> comparable</i>)

<li>justified</li></ol>
